restore=: && backupdir=".am$$" && \
rm -rf $backupdir && mkdir $backupdir && \
if (true true true --version) >/dev/null 2>&1; then \
  for f in doc/as.info doc/as.info-[0-9] doc/as.info-[0-9][0-9] doc/as.i[0-9] doc/as.i[0-9][0-9]; do \
    if test -f $f; then mv $f $backupdir; restore=mv; else :; fi; \
  done; \
else :; fi && \
if true true true -I "/var/tmp/portage/sys-devel/binutils-2.42-r2/work/binutils-2.42/gas/doc" -I doc -I "/var/tmp/portage/sys-devel/binutils-2.42-r2/work/binutils-2.42/gas/../libiberty" -I "/var/tmp/portage/sys-devel/binutils-2.42-r2/work/binutils-2.42/gas/../bfd/doc" -I ../bfd/doc --no-split  -I doc -I /var/tmp/portage/sys-devel/binutils-2.42-r2/work/binutils-2.42/gas/doc \

then \
  rc=0; \
else \
  rc=$?; \
  $restore $backupdir/* `echo "./doc/as.info" | sed 's|[^/]*$||'`; \
fi; \

    k=`echo $j | sed 's,y,y,'`; \
